function AD takes nothing returns nothing
local trigger UD
local playerunitevent ID
local integer PD
set vi=CreateTrigger()
set UD=vi
set ID=EVENT_PLAYER_UNIT_UPGRADE_FINISH
set PD=0
loop
call TriggerRegisterPlayerUnitEvent(UD,Player(PD),ID,null)
set PD=PD+1
exitwhen PD==bj_MAX_PLAYER_SLOTS
endloop
call TriggerAddCondition(vi,Condition(ha))
call TriggerAddAction(vi,Fa)
set UD=null
set ID=null
endfunction

endfunction

function AF takes nothing returns nothing
local player jF=GetOwningPlayer(GetSpellTargetUnit())
local playerstate xF=PLAYER_STATE_RESOURCE_GOLD
local playerstate vF
local playerstate mF
local player QF
local force WF
local location EF
local real ZF
local real UF
local player IF
local force PF
if xF==PLAYER_STATE_RESOURCE_GOLD then
set vF=PLAYER_STATE_GOLD_GATHERED
call SetPlayerState(jF,vF,GetPlayerState(jF,vF)+500)
elseif xF==PLAYER_STATE_RESOURCE_LUMBER then
set mF=PLAYER_STATE_LUMBER_GATHERED
call SetPlayerState(jF,mF,GetPlayerState(jF,mF)+500)
endif
call SetPlayerState(jF,xF,GetPlayerState(jF,xF)+500)
call RemoveUnit(GetSpellAbilityUnit())
set QF=GetOwningPlayer(GetSpellTargetUnit())
set WF=CreateForce()
call ForceAddPlayer(WF,QF)
if IsPlayerInForce(GetLocalPlayer(),WF) then
call DisplayTextToPlayer(GetLocalPlayer(),0.,0.,"TRIGSTR_1231")
endif
set y=GetUnitLoc(GetSpellTargetUnit())
set IF=GetOwningPlayer(GetSpellTargetUnit())
set PF=CreateForce()
call ForceAddPlayer(PF,IF)
set EF=y
set ZF=GetLocationX(EF)
set UF=GetLocationY(EF)
if IsPlayerInForce(GetLocalPlayer(),PF) then
call PingMinimap(ZF,UF,2.00)
endif
call RemoveLocation(y)
set jF=null
set xF=null
set vF=null
set mF=null
set QF=null
set WF=null
set EF=null
set IF=null
set PF=null
endfunction

function dSw takes integer nSw returns string
if nSw==0 then
return "|cffADADADtrace|r"
elseif nSw==1 then
return "|cff2685DCdebug|r"
elseif nSw==2 then
return "|cffFFCC00info|r"
elseif nSw==3 then
return "|cffF47E3Ewarning|r"
elseif nSw==4 then
return "|cffFB2700error|r"
endif
return "?"
endfunction
function W6 takes string G6,string g6 returns nothing
local integer h6
local integer F6
local integer k6
local string j6
local integer x6
local integer v6
local string m6
local string Q6
set Wb[Qb]=g6
set Qb=Qb+1
set h6=StringHash(G6)
if HaveSavedInteger(Kc,-1,h6) then
if LoadInteger(Kc,-1,h6)+60<ro then
set m6=G6
set g6=""
set F6=Qb
set k6=0
loop
set F6=F6-1
set k6=k6+1
exitwhen k6>20 or F6<0
set g6=g6+"\n   "+Wb[F6]
endloop
call DisplayTimedTextToPlayer(fO,0.,0.,45.,dSw(4)+" - "+m6+g6)
call SaveInteger(Kc,-1,h6,R2I(ro))
call SaveBoolean(Kc,-1,h6,false)
elseif HaveSavedBoolean(Kc,-1,h6) then
if not LoadBoolean(Kc,-1,h6) then
call DisplayTimedTextToPlayer(fO,0.,0.,45.,dSw(4)+" - "+"|cffFF3A29Excessive repeating errors are being omitted")
call SaveBoolean(Kc,-1,h6,true)
endif
else
call DisplayTimedTextToPlayer(fO,0.,0.,45.,dSw(4)+" - "+"|cffFF3A29Excessive repeating errors are being omitted")
call SaveBoolean(Kc,-1,h6,true)
endif
else
call SaveInteger(Kc,-1,h6,R2I(ro))
set Q6="Message: "+G6
set j6=""
set x6=Qb
set v6=0
loop
set x6=x6-1
set v6=v6+1
exitwhen v6>20 or x6<0
set j6=j6+"\n   "+Wb[x6]
endloop
call DisplayTimedTextToPlayer(fO,0.,0.,45.,dSw(4)+" - "+Q6+j6)
endif
call I2S(1/0)
set Qb=Qb-1
endfunction
function l7 takes string o7 returns integer
local integer O7
set Wb[Qb]=o7
set Qb=Qb+1
set Wb[Qb]="when calling HashMap in HashMap, line 7"
set Qb=Qb+1
if ib==0 then
if Sb<32768 then
set Sb=Sb+1
set O7=Sb
set cb[O7]=727
else
call W6("Out of memory: Could not create HashMap.","when calling error in HashMap, line 8")
set O7=0
endif
else
set ib=ib-1
set O7=tb[ib]
set cb[O7]=727
endif
set Qb=Qb-1-1
return O7
endfunction
function pcw takes playerunitevent tcw,code icw,code Scw,code ccw returns nothing
local integer ocw=GetHandleId(tcw)
local integer Ocw
local filterfunc lcw
local trigger bcw
local player ycw
if vO[ocw]==null then
set vO[ocw]=CreateTrigger()
set Ocw=bj_MAX_PLAYER_SLOTS-1
loop
exitwhen Ocw<0
set bcw=vO[ocw]
set ycw=dO[Ocw]
if icw!=null then
set lcw=Filter(icw)
else
set lcw=null
endif
call TriggerRegisterPlayerUnitEvent(bcw,ycw,tcw,lcw)
set Ocw=Ocw-1
endloop
endif
if Scw!=null then
call TriggerAddCondition(vO[ocw],Filter(Scw))
endif
if ccw!=null then
call TriggerAddAction(vO[ocw],ccw)
endif
set lcw=null
set bcw=null
set ycw=null
endfunction
function Aaw takes nothing returns boolean
set Qb=0
set Wb[Qb]="RegisterEvents, line 1"
set Qb=Qb+1
set mO=l7("when calling new_HashMap in RegisterEvents, line 55")
call pcw(EVENT_PLAYER_UNIT_SPELL_EFFECT,null,xf,null)
set Qb=Qb-1
return true
endfunction

function Ak takes nothing returns nothing
local player jk=GetOwningPlayer(GetKillingUnit())
local playerstate xk=PLAYER_STATE_RESOURCE_GOLD
local playerstate vk
local playerstate mk
local player Qk
local force Wk
local location Ek
local real Zk
local real Uk
local player Ik
local force Pk
if xk==PLAYER_STATE_RESOURCE_GOLD then
set vk=PLAYER_STATE_GOLD_GATHERED
call SetPlayerState(jk,vk,GetPlayerState(jk,vk)+125)
elseif xk==PLAYER_STATE_RESOURCE_LUMBER then
set mk=PLAYER_STATE_LUMBER_GATHERED
call SetPlayerState(jk,mk,GetPlayerState(jk,mk)+125)
endif
call SetPlayerState(jk,xk,GetPlayerState(jk,xk)+125)
set Qk=GetOwningPlayer(GetKillingUnit())
set Wk=CreateForce()
call ForceAddPlayer(Wk,Qk)
if IsPlayerInForce(GetLocalPlayer(),Wk) then
call DisplayTextToPlayer(GetLocalPlayer(),0.,0.,"TRIGSTR_091")
endif
set y=GetUnitLoc(GetDyingUnit())
set Ik=GetOwningPlayer(GetDyingUnit())
set Pk=CreateForce()
call ForceAddPlayer(Pk,Ik)
set Ek=y
set Zk=GetLocationX(Ek)
set Uk=GetLocationY(Ek)
if IsPlayerInForce(GetLocalPlayer(),Pk) then
call PingMinimap(Zk,Uk,2.00)
endif
call RemoveLocation(y)
set jk=null
set xk=null
set vk=null
set mk=null
set Qk=null
set Wk=null
set Ek=null
set Ik=null
set Pk=null

function Qg takes nothing returns nothing
local location Gg
local location gg
local real hg
local real Fg
local rect kg
local group jg
local group xg
local code vg
local boolean mg
set u=GetUnitLoc(GetSpellAbilityUnit())
set Gg=u
set c=Location(GetLocationX(Gg)+200.00,GetLocationY(Gg)+0.00)
set gg=u
set hg=GetLocationX(gg)
set Fg=GetLocationY(gg)
set O=Rect(hg-150,Fg-140,hg+150,Fg+140)
set kg=O
set jg=CreateGroup()
call GroupEnumUnitsInRect(jg,kg,null)
call DestroyBoolExpr(null)
set l=jg
set xg=l
set vg=Dy
set mg=bj_wantDestroyGroup
set bj_wantDestroyGroup=false
call ForGroup(xg,vg)
if mg then
call DestroyGroup(xg)
endif
call ReplaceUnitBJ(GetSpellAbilityUnit(),1747988826,bj_UNIT_STATE_METHOD_RELATIVE)
call SetUnitAnimation(bj_lastReplacedUnit,"stand")
call DestroyGroup(l)
call RemoveLocation(c)
call RemoveLocation(u)
set Gg=null
set gg=null
set kg=null
set jg=null
set xg=null
endfunction

function RF takes nothing returns nothing
local player OF=GetOwningPlayer(GetSpellTargetUnit())
local playerstate lF=PLAYER_STATE_RESOURCE_GOLD
local playerstate bF
local playerstate yF
local player pF
local force eF
local location qF
local real aF
local real nF
local player dF
local force fF
if lF==PLAYER_STATE_RESOURCE_GOLD then
set bF=PLAYER_STATE_GOLD_GATHERED
call SetPlayerState(OF,bF,GetPlayerState(OF,bF)+250)
elseif lF==PLAYER_STATE_RESOURCE_LUMBER then
set yF=PLAYER_STATE_LUMBER_GATHERED
call SetPlayerState(OF,yF,GetPlayerState(OF,yF)+250)
endif
call SetPlayerState(OF,lF,GetPlayerState(OF,lF)+250)
call RemoveUnit(GetSpellAbilityUnit())
set pF=GetOwningPlayer(GetSpellTargetUnit())
set eF=CreateForce()
call ForceAddPlayer(eF,pF)
if IsPlayerInForce(GetLocalPlayer(),eF) then
call DisplayTextToPlayer(GetLocalPlayer(),0.,0.,"TRIGSTR_1230")
endif
set y=GetUnitLoc(GetSpellTargetUnit())
set dF=GetOwningPlayer(GetSpellTargetUnit())
set fF=CreateForce()
call ForceAddPlayer(fF,dF)
set qF=y
set aF=GetLocationX(qF)
set nF=GetLocationY(qF)
if IsPlayerInForce(GetLocalPlayer(),fF) then
call PingMinimap(aF,nF,2.00)
endif
call RemoveLocation(y)
set OF=null
set lF=null
set bF=null
set yF=null
set pF=null
set eF=null
set qF=null
set dF=null
set fF=null
endfunction

function TD takes nothing returns nothing
local integer eD=1
local integer qD=1751868773
local player aD=GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit())
local rect RD=bj_mapInitialPlayableArea
local location fD=Location(GetRectCenterX(RD),GetRectCenterY(RD))
local location nD=Location(GetLocationX(fD)+100000000.00,GetLocationY(fD)+100000000.00)
local real dD=bj_UNIT_FACING
call GroupClear(bj_lastCreatedGroup)
loop
set eD=eD-1
exitwhen eD<0
call CreateUnitAtLocSaveLast(aD,qD,nD,dD)
call GroupAddUnit(bj_lastCreatedGroup,bj_lastCreatedUnit)
endloop
call ShowUnit(bj_lastCreatedUnit,false)
set aD=null
set nD=null
set fD=null
set RD=null
endfunction

set r1=s1
exitwhen true
endif
set s1=s1+1
endloop
if r1<=23 then
set i1=B3
set S1=0
set c1=0
set o1=bj_MAX_PLAYER_SLOTS-1
loop
exitwhen c1>o1
if gO[c1]==i1 then
set S1=c1
exitwhen true
endif
set c1=c1+1
endloop
set N3=jc[S1]
set M3=xc[S1]
set w1=vc[S1]
else
set N3=0
set M3=0
set w1=0
endif
set Eb=N3
set Zb=M3
set Ub=w1
set u1=null
set i1=null
return Eb
endfunction
function V3 takes player D3 returns string
local integer L3=O1(GetPlayerColor(D3))
local integer X3=Zb
local integer C3=Ub
local integer H3=L3/16
local integer J3=X3/16
local integer K3=C3/16
return "|cff"+mc[H3]+mc[L3-H3*16]+mc[J3]+mc[X3-J3*16]+mc[K3]+mc[C3-K3*16]+GetPlayerName(D3)+"|r"
endfunction

function Wh takes nothing returns nothing
local player Yh=GetOwningPlayer(GetSpellTargetUnit())
local playerstate Gh=PLAYER_STATE_RESOURCE_LUMBER
local playerstate gh
local playerstate hh
local player Fh
local force kh
local location jh
local real xh
local real vh
local player mh
local force Qh
if Gh==PLAYER_STATE_RESOURCE_GOLD then
set gh=PLAYER_STATE_GOLD_GATHERED
call SetPlayerState(Yh,gh,GetPlayerState(Yh,gh)+250)
elseif Gh==PLAYER_STATE_RESOURCE_LUMBER then
set hh=PLAYER_STATE_LUMBER_GATHERED
call SetPlayerState(Yh,hh,GetPlayerState(Yh,hh)+250)
endif
call SetPlayerState(Yh,Gh,GetPlayerState(Yh,Gh)+250)
call RemoveUnit(GetSpellAbilityUnit())
set Fh=GetOwningPlayer(GetSpellTargetUnit())
set kh=CreateForce()
call ForceAddPlayer(kh,Fh)
if IsPlayerInForce(GetLocalPlayer(),kh) then
call DisplayTextToPlayer(GetLocalPlayer(),0.,0.,"TRIGSTR_1229")
endif
set y=GetUnitLoc(GetSpellTargetUnit())
set mh=GetOwningPlayer(GetSpellTargetUnit())
set Qh=CreateForce()
call ForceAddPlayer(Qh,mh)
set jh=y
set xh=GetLocationX(jh)
set vh=GetLocationY(jh)
if IsPlayerInForce(GetLocalPlayer(),Qh) then
call PingMinimap(xh,vh,2.00)
endif
call RemoveLocation(y)
set Yh=null
set Gh=null
set gh=null
set hh=null
set Fh=null
set kh=null
set jh=null
set mh=null
set Qh=null
endfunction

function jww takes real Gww,real gww,real hww,real Fww,real kww returns real
set hww=GetRandomReal(hww,Fww)
return (Gww+gww)/2.+Yww(hww)*Pow(2.718281828,-(Pow(hww,2.)/2.*kww))/SquareRoot(6.283185482*kww)*((gww-Gww)/2.)
endfunction

endfunction

return true
endfunction

function gj takes nothing returns nothing
local player pj=GetOwningPlayer(GetSpellTargetUnit())
local playerstate ej=PLAYER_STATE_RESOURCE_LUMBER
local playerstate qj
local playerstate aj
local player nj
local force dj
local location fj
local real Rj
local real Tj
local player Yj
local force Gj
if ej==PLAYER_STATE_RESOURCE_GOLD then
set qj=PLAYER_STATE_GOLD_GATHERED
call SetPlayerState(pj,qj,GetPlayerState(pj,qj)+500)
elseif ej==PLAYER_STATE_RESOURCE_LUMBER then
set aj=PLAYER_STATE_LUMBER_GATHERED
call SetPlayerState(pj,aj,GetPlayerState(pj,aj)+500)
endif
call SetPlayerState(pj,ej,GetPlayerState(pj,ej)+500)
call RemoveUnit(GetSpellAbilityUnit())
set nj=GetOwningPlayer(GetSpellTargetUnit())
set dj=CreateForce()
call ForceAddPlayer(dj,nj)
if IsPlayerInForce(GetLocalPlayer(),dj) then
call DisplayTextToPlayer(GetLocalPlayer(),0.,0.,"TRIGSTR_1232")
endif
set y=GetUnitLoc(GetSpellTargetUnit())
set Yj=GetOwningPlayer(GetSpellTargetUnit())
set Gj=CreateForce()
call ForceAddPlayer(Gj,Yj)
set fj=y
set Rj=GetLocationX(fj)
set Tj=GetLocationY(fj)
if IsPlayerInForce(GetLocalPlayer(),Gj) then
call PingMinimap(Rj,Tj,2.00)
endif
call RemoveLocation(y)
set pj=null
set ej=null
set qj=null
set aj=null
set nj=null
set dj=null
set fj=null
set Yj=null
set Gj=null
endfunction

function ulw takes unit COw,unit VOw returns real
local real BOw=GetUnitX(COw)
local real NOw=GetUnitY(COw)
local real MOw=BOw-GetUnitX(VOw)
local real wlw=NOw-GetUnitY(VOw)
return SquareRoot(MOw*MOw+wlw*wlw)
endfunction

function qL takes integer MK,string wL returns nothing
local unit uL
local player rL
local integer sL
local integer tL
local boolean iL
local unit SL
local integer cL
local boolean oL
local real OL
local boolean lL
local integer bL
local real yL
local real pL
local real eL
set Wb[Qb]=wL
set Qb=Qb+1
set uL=GetTriggerUnit()
set sL=ql
set tL=GetUnitTypeId(uL)
set Wb[Qb]="when calling has in CastleCapture, line 11"
set Qb=Qb+1
if Tb[sL]==0 then
if sL==0 then
call W6("Nullpointer exception when calling LinkedList.has","when calling error in LinkedList, line 103")
else
call W6("Called LinkedList.has on invalid object.","when calling error in LinkedList, line 103")
endif
endif
set iL=S9(sL,tL)
set Qb=Qb-1
if iL then
if GetUnitStatePercent(uL,UNIT_STATE_LIFE,UNIT_STATE_MAX_LIFE)<=50.0 then
set oL=GetOwningPlayer(uL)!=GetOwningPlayer(GetAttacker())
else
set oL=false
endif
if oL then
set OL=GetUnitX(uL)
set yL=GetUnitY(uL)
set SL=GetAttacker()
set pL=OL-GetUnitX(SL)
set eL=yL-GetUnitY(SL)
set lL=SquareRoot(pL*pL+eL*eL)<=300.0
else
set lL=false
endif
if lL then
set rL=GetOwningPlayer(GetAttacker())
call SetUnitOwner(uL,rL,true)
if GetPlayerId(rL)!=PLAYER_NEUTRAL_AGGRESSIVE then
set bL=fC(GetUnitTypeId(uL))
set cL=yO[GetPlayerId(rL)]
set Wb[Qb]="when calling getForceId in CastleCapture, line 17"
set Qb=Qb+1
if kb[cL]==0 then
if cL==0 then
call W6("Nullpointer exception when calling PlayerStats.getForceId","when calling error in PlayerStats, line 94")
else
call W6("Called PlayerStats.getForceId on invalid object.","when calling error in PlayerStats, line 94")
endif
endif
set MK=pO[cL]
set Qb=Qb-1
call ReplaceUnitBJ(uL,YC(bL,MK),bj_UNIT_STATE_METHOD_RELATIVE)
endif
call SetUnitState(uL,UNIT_STATE_LIFE,GetUnitState(uL,UNIT_STATE_MAX_LIFE)*RMaxBJ(0.,60.0)*0.01)
call SetUnitState(uL,UNIT_STATE_MANA,GetUnitState(uL,UNIT_STATE_MAX_MANA)*RMaxBJ(0.,0.0)*0.01)
call UnitAddAbility(uL,1093677896)
endif
endif
set Qb=Qb-1
set uL=null
set rL=null
set SL=null
endfunction

function ij takes nothing returns nothing
local player Xk=GetOwningPlayer(GetKillingUnit())
local playerstate Ck=PLAYER_STATE_RESOURCE_GOLD
local playerstate Vk
local playerstate Bk
local player Nk
local force Mk
local location wj
local real uj
local real rj
local player sj
local force tj
if Ck==PLAYER_STATE_RESOURCE_GOLD then
set Vk=PLAYER_STATE_GOLD_GATHERED
call SetPlayerState(Xk,Vk,GetPlayerState(Xk,Vk)+250)
elseif Ck==PLAYER_STATE_RESOURCE_LUMBER then
set Bk=PLAYER_STATE_LUMBER_GATHERED
call SetPlayerState(Xk,Bk,GetPlayerState(Xk,Bk)+250)
endif
call SetPlayerState(Xk,Ck,GetPlayerState(Xk,Ck)+250)
set Nk=GetOwningPlayer(GetKillingUnit())
set Mk=CreateForce()
call ForceAddPlayer(Mk,Nk)
if IsPlayerInForce(GetLocalPlayer(),Mk) then
call DisplayTextToPlayer(GetLocalPlayer(),0.,0.,"TRIGSTR_092")
endif
set y=GetUnitLoc(GetDyingUnit())
set sj=GetOwningPlayer(GetDyingUnit())
set tj=CreateForce()
call ForceAddPlayer(tj,sj)
set wj=y
set uj=GetLocationX(wj)
set rj=GetLocationY(wj)
if IsPlayerInForce(GetLocalPlayer(),tj) then
call PingMinimap(uj,rj,2.00)
endif
call RemoveLocation(y)
set Xk=null
set Ck=null
set Vk=null
set Bk=null
set Nk=null
set Mk=null
set wj=null
set sj=null
set tj=null
endfunction

function kx takes nothing returns nothing
local player ax=GetOwningPlayer(GetKillingUnit())
local playerstate nx=PLAYER_STATE_RESOURCE_LUMBER
local playerstate dx
local playerstate fx
local player Rx
local force Tx
local location Yx
local real Gx
local real gx
local player hx
local force Fx
if nx==PLAYER_STATE_RESOURCE_GOLD then
set dx=PLAYER_STATE_GOLD_GATHERED
call SetPlayerState(ax,dx,GetPlayerState(ax,dx)+500)
elseif nx==PLAYER_STATE_RESOURCE_LUMBER then
set fx=PLAYER_STATE_LUMBER_GATHERED
call SetPlayerState(ax,fx,GetPlayerState(ax,fx)+500)
endif
call SetPlayerState(ax,nx,GetPlayerState(ax,nx)+500)
set Rx=GetOwningPlayer(GetKillingUnit())
set Tx=CreateForce()
call ForceAddPlayer(Tx,Rx)
if IsPlayerInForce(GetLocalPlayer(),Tx) then
call DisplayTextToPlayer(GetLocalPlayer(),0.,0.,"TRIGSTR_084")
endif
set y=GetUnitLoc(GetDyingUnit())
set hx=GetOwningPlayer(GetDyingUnit())
set Fx=CreateForce()
call ForceAddPlayer(Fx,hx)
set Yx=y
set Gx=GetLocationX(Yx)
set gx=GetLocationY(Yx)
if IsPlayerInForce(GetLocalPlayer(),Fx) then
call PingMinimap(Gx,gx,2.00)
endif
call RemoveLocation(y)
set ax=null
set nx=null
set dx=null
set fx=null
set Rx=null
set Tx=null
set Yx=null
set hx=null
set Fx=null
endfunction

function uF takes nothing returns nothing
local player Hh=GetOwningPlayer(GetSpellTargetUnit())
local playerstate Jh=PLAYER_STATE_RESOURCE_LUMBER
local playerstate Kh
local playerstate Lh
local player Xh
local force Ch
local location Vh
local real Bh
local real Nh
local player Mh
local force wF
if Jh==PLAYER_STATE_RESOURCE_GOLD then
set Kh=PLAYER_STATE_GOLD_GATHERED
call SetPlayerState(Hh,Kh,GetPlayerState(Hh,Kh)+500)
elseif Jh==PLAYER_STATE_RESOURCE_LUMBER then
set Lh=PLAYER_STATE_LUMBER_GATHERED
call SetPlayerState(Hh,Lh,GetPlayerState(Hh,Lh)+500)
endif
call SetPlayerState(Hh,Jh,GetPlayerState(Hh,Jh)+500)
call RemoveUnit(GetSpellAbilityUnit())
set Xh=GetOwningPlayer(GetSpellTargetUnit())
set Ch=CreateForce()
call ForceAddPlayer(Ch,Xh)
if IsPlayerInForce(GetLocalPlayer(),Ch) then
call DisplayTextToPlayer(GetLocalPlayer(),0.,0.,"TRIGSTR_1228")
endif
set y=GetUnitLoc(GetSpellTargetUnit())
set Mh=GetOwningPlayer(GetSpellTargetUnit())
set wF=CreateForce()
call ForceAddPlayer(wF,Mh)
set Vh=y
set Bh=GetLocationX(Vh)
set Nh=GetLocationY(Vh)
if IsPlayerInForce(GetLocalPlayer(),wF) then
call PingMinimap(Bh,Nh,2.00)
endif
call RemoveLocation(y)
set Hh=null
set Jh=null
set Kh=null
set Lh=null
set Xh=null
set Ch=null
set Vh=null
set Mh=null
set wF=null
endfunction
